24-27 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [PRO TOUR KALADESH](/en/events/coverage/ptkld)
 on October 16, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast











Twenty-Four players earned 24 point or more from their Standard rounds at Pro Tour *Kaladesh*. Seventeen of those players hit exactly 24 points (8-2), two players received 25 points (8-1-1), one player received got to 26 points (8-0-2), and four players received 27 points (9-1).




---

**The following players finished with 27 points (9-1) in Standard:**







#### Hatto, Steve - Blue-White Midrange


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
